The position of a cell in the skill tree sheets determines its position in the skill screen UI. 
The format for the cells is: [SKILL_ID],[PARENT0_SKILL_ID], [PARENT1_SKILL_ID]
Each skill can have 0-2 parents, but only the top nodes should have 0 parents.
